  //guardar cookie de la compra
	function modificarCookieSeguimiento(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
	    var d = new Date();
	    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
	    var expires = "expires = "+d.toGMTString(); 
	    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + " ; " + expires+"; path=/; domain=.homecenter.com.co";
	}
  
  function getCookieInfoFinal(cname){
		var name = cname + "=";
    	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    	for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
        	var c = ca[i];
        	while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
        	if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    	}
    	return "";
	}
  
  function getCookieSeguimiento(cname){
      var name = cname + "=";
      var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
      for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
         var c = ca[i];
         while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
         if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
      }
      return "";
    } 
  
  /*obtener  sku de producto desde la url*/	
	function $_GET(param){
		/* Obtener la url completa */
		url = document.URL;
		/* Buscar a partir del signo de interrogación ? */
		url = String(url.match(/\?+.+/));
		/* limpiar la cadena quitándole el signo ? */
		url = url.replace("?", "");
		/* Crear un array con parametro=valor */
		url = url.split("&");
		/*
		Recorrer el array url
		obtener el valor y dividirlo en dos partes a través del signo =
		0 = parametro
		1 = valor
		Si el parámetro existe devolver su valor
		*/
		x = 0;
		while (x < url.length)
		{
			p = url[x].split("=");
			if (p[0] == param)
			{
				return decodeURIComponent(p[1]);
			}
		x++;
		}
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $("#group").mouseover("mouseenter", function() {
            timer = setTimeout(function() {
                $("#group-content").show();
                $("#addBold").addClass("addBold");
            }, 350);
        });

        $("#group").on("mouseout", function() {
            clearInterval(timer);
        });

        $(".grupoSection").mouseleave(function() {
            $(".grupoSection").hide();
            $("#addBold").removeClass("addBold");

        });
    });
</script>

            contenedor.style.visibility = 'hidden';
            contenedor.style.opacity = '0';

    });

     <script type="text/javascript" language="javascript">
    /*
    You can use below ways to define rule.
    1. "checkName" : {"msg":"your error message"}.
    2. "checkName" : {"regex":"your regex expression","msg":"your error message"}.
    
    For 1, you should add the mapping into validator.funMapping, such as:
        validator.funMapping["your checkName"]= your check method for this check name.
    	validator.funMapping["test"]=validator.checkTest;
    	In the jsp, you can use it like this.  class="validate[test]"
    	
    For 2. You only need to use it in the jsp like this. class="custom[checkName]".
    
    For1 & 2, you can add a special error/success message render function. Sample:
        "required" : {
            (required)"msg" : "error message",
            (optional)"regex" : "your regex expression",
    		(optional)"succCall" : validator.requiredSuccCall,
    		(optional)"errorCall" : validator.requiredErrorCall
        }
    */

	<script id="ebOneTagUrlId" src="https://secure-ds.serving-sys.com/SemiCachedScripts/ebOneTag.js"></script><script>
	function setRecommendation_Interaction(experimentId, recommendationId, sku, description, eventAction = "click") {
		var now = getDateTime();

		exponea.track("recommendation_interaction", {
			experiment_id: experimentId,
			recommendation_id: recommendationId,
			interaction_date: now,
			event: eventAction,
			sku: sku,
			description: description
		});
	};
	
	function getDateTime() {
		var current_datetime = new Date();
		
		var current_datetime_day = (current_datetime.getDate() < 10) ? '0' + current_datetime.getDate() : current_datetime.getDate();
		var current_datetime_month = ((current_datetime.getMonth() +1) < 10) ? '0' + (current_datetime.getMonth() + 1) : current_datetime.getMonth() + 1;

		var current_datetime_hour = (current_datetime.getHours() < 10) ? '0' + current_datetime.getHours() : current_datetime.getHours();
		var current_datetime_minute = (current_datetime.getMinutes() < 10) ? '0' + current_datetime.getMinutes() : current_datetime.getMinutes();
		var current_datetime_second = (current_datetime.getSeconds() < 10) ? '0' + current_datetime.getSeconds() : current_datetime.getSeconds();


		var dateTime = current_datetime.getFullYear() + "-" + current_datetime_month + "-" + current_datetime_day + " " + current_datetime_hour + ":" + current_datetime_minute + ":" + current_datetime_second;

		return dateTime;
	}

			});

			clearInterval(intervalosEncuesta);
		}
	}, 1000);
});

  function getCookieInfemailMD5(cname){
		var name = cname + "=";
    	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    	for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
        	var c = ca[i];
        	while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
        	if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
    	}
    	return "";
	}

  function eliminarCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
	    var d = new Date();
	    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
	    var expires = "expires = "+d.toGMTString(); 
	    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + " ; " + expires+"; path=/; domain=.homecenter.com.co";
	}

var cartExponea = localStorage.getItem('cart_exponea') ? JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart_exponea')) : { cart: [], totalPrice: 0, totalQuantity: 0 };

function addToCartInExponea(){
	setTimeout(function(){
		console.log('se ejecuta la funcion addToCartInExponea 19');
		$('.item-list.filStyleCar').each(function () {
			var item = $(this);
			item.find('.btn.btn-default.bootstrap-touchspin-up').click(function () {
				if (item.find('.caractInfoStyle').length > 0) {
					console.log('sumar producto : ', item.find('.caractInfoStyle').text().replace('SKU:', '').trim());
					var exist = 0;
					var iteration;
					for(var i = 0; i < cartExponea.cart.length; i++){
						if(cartExponea.cart[i].item_id == item.find('.caractInfoStyle').text().replace('SKU:', '').trim()){
							exist++;
							iteration = i;
							i = cartExponea.cart.length;
						}
					}
					if(exist == 0){
						console.log('no hay repetidos');
						cartExponea.cart.push({
							item_id: item.find('.caractInfoStyle').text().replace('SKU:', '').trim(),
							quantity: 1
						});
						var price = 0;
						var categoryId = '';
						for(var j = 0; j < digitalData.ecom.productList.length; j++){
							if(digitalData.ecom.productList[j].sku == item.find('.caractInfoStyle').text().replace('SKU:', '').trim()){
								price = digitalData.ecom.productList[j].price;
								categoryId = digitalData.ecom.productList[j].category;
								j = digitalData.ecom.productList.length;
							}
						}
						cartExponea.totalPrice += price;
						cartExponea.totalQuantity++;

						console.log('nombre sku exponea', item.find('.bold-text.pb-10').text());
						console.log('categoryId', categoryId);

						var objExponea = {
							'items': JSON.stringify(cartExponea.cart),
							'action': 'add',
							'item_id': item.find('.caractInfoStyle').text().replace('SKU:', '').trim(),
							'item_sku': item.find('.caractInfoStyle').text().replace('SKU:', '').trim(),
							'item_price': price,
							'item_name': item.find('.bold-text.pb-10').text(),
							'category_id': categoryId,
							'category_name': '',
							'item_quantity': 1,
							'total_price': cartExponea.totalPrice,
							'total_quantity': cartExponea.totalQuantity
						};

						console.log('objExponea: ', objExponea);

						exponea.track('cart_update', objExponea);
					}
					else{
						console.log('si hay repetidos');
						var quantityTemp = cartExponea.cart[iteration].quantity;
						cartExponea.cart[iteration] = {
							item_id: item.find('.caractInfoStyle').text().replace('SKU:', '').trim(),
							quantity: quantityTemp + 1
						};
						var price = 0;

						console.log('categoryId', categoryId);

							'items': JSON.stringify(cartExponea.cart),

									'item_sku': item.find('.caractInfoStyle').text().replace('SKU:', '').trim(),

							}
							i = cartExponea.cart.length;
						}
					}
				} else if (item.find('.pb-10').length) {
					console.log('restar producto : ', item.find('.pb-10').last().text().replace('SKU:', '').trim());
					for(var i = 0; i < cartExponea.cart.length; i++){
						console.log('iteracion ', i);
						if(cartExponea.cart[i].item_id == item.find('.pb-10').last().text().replace('SKU:', '').trim()){
							console.log('para en ', cartExponea.cart[i]);
							if(cartExponea.cart[i].quantity > 1){
								console.log('hay mas de uno');
								var quantityTemp = cartExponea.cart[i].quantity
								cartExponea.cart[i] = {
									item_id: item.find('.pb-10').last().text().replace('SKU:', '').trim(),
									quantity: quantityTemp - 1
								};
								var price = 0;
								var categoryId = '';
								for(var j = 0; j < digitalData.ecom.productList.length; j++){
									if(digitalData.ecom.productList[j].sku == item.find('.pb-10').last().text().replace('SKU:', '').trim()){
										price = digitalData.ecom.productList[j].price;
										categoryId = digitalData.ecom.productList[j].category;
										j = digitalData.ecom.productList.length;
									}
								}
								cartExponea.totalPrice -= price;
								cartExponea.totalQuantity--;

								console.log('nombre sku exponea', item.find('.bold-text.pb-10').text());
								console.log('categoryId', categoryId);

									'items': JSON.stringify(cartExponea.cart),
